"npc_dota_hero_antimage_bio"	"Th' monks o' Turstarkuri were a-watchin' th' rugged valleys layin' below their mountain, all while invaders were forcin' themselves through th' kingdoms down thar. They were thinkin' men, these monks, lookin' at all th' fightin' as from a bird's eye, wrapped up in their thinkin' an' musin' that won't think of no gods, or no magic. Up in their little hole, they kept themselves apart--above--all th' warrin' at their doorstep. Then along came th' Legion o' th' Dead God. Crusaders, they were, o' a mind t' see all th' local worshippin' replaced wit' their own Unliving Lord's poisonous non-thinkin' ways--\"nihilosophy\", as it be. In that place what had thought naught but o' blood and battle fer o'er a thousand years' time, they tore at th' very souls an' bones of them who'd gone and died afore 'em an' had them pitched against Turstarkuri. The monks scarcely stood a fortnight against th', an' the few monks who even bother'd t' look aroun' from their meditation-thinkin' what thought th' invaders were but visions o' demons, sent t' distract them from their thinkin'. They died right then an' there, sittin' as they were on their silken cushions, save one youth--a pilgrim who'd made 'is way there as an acolyte seekin' wisdom, yet hadn't been made one o' them right proper. He watch'd there, the boy's face all twisted in horror as th' monks he'd been servin' tea an' th' like t' were slaughtered an' raised from th' dead in th' same hour t' ally 'emselves among th' ranks of th' Dead God's own. Wit' naught but a few o' Turstarkuri's prized scrolls, th' boy made his way fer safer lands, makin' an oath t' himself: t' obliterate not only the Dead God's own sorcerer folk--but t' put an end to all th' magic thar be. "

"npc_dota_hero_queenofpain_bio"	"Th' Ecclesiast-King o' Elze basked in th' nature o' pain--ghastly pain. In a less powerful leader, such desires might be kept under wraps, but in a king o' his status, t' satisfy such thirsts would have endanger'd th' virtue o' th' Divine Throne itself. So he turn'd t' his dungeon full o' demon masters, promisin' freedom t' whoever could conjure a personal succubus o' sufferin' an' bind it fully t' his service. Th' creature who was conjured, Akasha by name, grant'd him such beloved torment that he called her his Secret Queen, an' he began t' spend his time enjoyin' her mighty sufferin'--eventually retirin' from th' throne in-exchange for th' pleasure o' th' Queen's pain. Queen o' Pain could bring him t' th' brink o' perishin', but she was forced t' keep him alive by th' demon code. At last th' King's neglectful pleasure led t' mutiny. He was dragg'd from his quarters an' hurled from th' Crow's Nest o' Invocations, and at th' moment o' his destruction, Queen o' Pain was let loose across th' seven seas, freed from her service--free t' inflict her nature upon any man (or woman) she desired."

"npc_dota_hero_lina_bio"	"Th' siblin' rivalries between Lina th' Slayer, an' her lil' lass Rylai, th' Crystal Maiden, were th' stuff o' pirate tales in th' cozy lands where they spent their landlubber years. Lina always had th' upperhand, however, for while Crystal was innocent an' simple, Lina's fiery nature was temper'd by cleverness an' cunnin'. Th' weary parents o' these rivals went through half a sailor's dozen towns, losin' one t' fire, th' other t' ice, before they figured life was best with th' youngin's apart. As th' oldest, Lina was sent t' th' southern seas t' live with a kindly aunt in th' fierce Desert o' Misrule, an area quite comfortable for th' flamin' Slayer. "npc_dota_hero_earthshaker_bio"	"Not so unlike a golem, or a gargoyle, Earthshaker were one wit' th' earth... but now walks atop it. Unlike many ano'er entity, this one make himself by virtue o' his own will, so servin' not a soul but 'imself. In 'is restless slumberin', encased deep in stone, he grew t' know o' th' life driftin' about their lives above him. He start'd a curious line o' thought, right then. Durin' a season o' tremors, th' Nishai peaks shook themselves a-loose o' avalanches, shiftin' th' course o' rivers and turnin' shallow valleys t' bottomless chasms. When th' land finally saw fit t' cease quakin', Earthshaker stepp'd from th' settlin' dust, tossin' aside massive boulders as if he were throwin' off seafoam. He'd shaped himself in th' image o' us mortals, so namin' 'imself Raigor Stonehoof. He bleeds now, an' breathes--he be as mortal as anyone, now. But that one's spirit still be that o' th' earth; he carries its power in th' magical totem that shan't be leavin' his side. An' on th' very day he returns t' dust, th' earth'll greet 'im as th' returnin' son that he be."

He were part o' th' crew lined up fer th' final assault 'gainst some nutter callin' himself \"Dread Magus Vorn\". Now they fought well, but not well enough, an' Azwraith 'imself were th' only survivior o' that fatal charge. Th' bloodshed made him furious, an' this in turn gave 'im focus. Armed wit' just his fishin' spear, he infiltrated th' keep, dispatchin' th' magick guardians an' dodgin' deadly traps. At th' top o' th' tower, Azwraith laid eyes upon th' villian bringin' chaos t' his homeland. Not a word were spoken 'tween th' two combatants as they duel'd through th' night. After hours, pike beat staff an' Azwraith pierced his foe. Now, magick be a curious beastie, an' as Vorn were struck he started t' glow wit' th' power o' a thousand suns. Suddenly he exploded, an' his power were absorbed by his killer. In th' aftermath o' it all, Azwraith found himself wit' th' company o' his own kin. Each dressed an' armed as he was, each thinkin' an' feelin' as he did. There was no time t' ponder such things - wit' th' magus defeated, a hearty roar o' victory sounded, an' footsteps rushed up th' tower t' cheer fer th' champion pikeman. He willed his new-found phantoms t' vanish, and so they did, one by one. When th' soldiers arrived, only a single lancer stood before them, who promptly vanished - he was just another phantom."

Kunkka's fleet was failin' hard, but in a move o' pure rum-filled fury Kunkka himself broke out th' hacks. Castin' tons o' overpowered all-critical witchcraft at th' demons he began t' wreck th' enemy. Oh, th' demons didn't see them comin'! But as th' gorefest wore on, nature used \"leet hacks\" o' its own. Th' waves rose up in towerin' spouts around th' few remaining ships, and Maelrawn th' Tentacular appeared amid th' fray. He chucked buckets o' rum at th' vessels, smashin' them into hearty-tastin' mounds. What th' proof o' that rum was, none can truly say. The Cataract roars off into th' void, deserted by its former deckhands. Kunkka now be Th' Admiral o' but one ship, a ghostly rig which endlessly replays the final seconds o' its destruction. How much rum was spilled overboard in th' crash remains a mystery 'till this very day."

Th' Grandmaster o' th' temple had hisself passed into Oblivion many a year ago, leavin' his academy wit'out a leader. From th' moment o' the'r master's heave t' Davy Jones' locker, th' regents o' th' temple began rites o' divination t' identify the'r master's reincarnation, an' wit' time, all signs pointed fer th' locals. Several villages were a-squattin' under th' temple, the'r alleys an' plazas full o' th' \"Yo ho ho\"in' o' tykes. Pugna, a wee thirteen months t' his name, were but one candidate among th' local brats, an' on th' appointed time he were presented at th' temple,  along wit' two other promisin' tots. Th' lamas offer'd a jumble o' worn relics t' th' children--booty o' the'r former grandmaster, it were. One lad reached fer a jewel-encrusted wand that'd belonged t' th' dead man...an' put 't up his nostril. A wee lass pulled ou' an amulet that'd also been th' dead man's, an' saw fit t' swallow 't, chain an' all! Pugna thought o' th' other tykes rather coolly, gave a merry, \"YO HO HO!\", an' blasted them wi' emerald flame, reducin' them t' ashes. The lad then snatched up th' wand an' amulet, claimin' his prizes. Th' regents promptly hoisted th' beamin' Pugna on the'r shoulders, wrapped th' lad up in the'r grandmaster's clothes, an' rushed th' lad t' th' keel 'afore his mood did any changin'. Not five year afterward, an' th' temple itself were ano'er pile o' ash, what made Pugna merry indeed."

"npc_dota_hero_omniknight_bio"	"Now, Purist Thunderwrath, he be a legendary fighter, blathering do-gooder an' a well-travelled pirate, sworn t' th' crew he were raised in. Brought up as a swab t' his reputed pirate elders, he spent his days livin' in fealty t' Ol' Mister One-Eye, Omniscience. T'were a \"Holy Struggle\", or so they say - I'd just call them scared dogs meself - never doubtin' th' orders o' his masters. But his elders died, as th' elderly be want t' do, an' were buried in sorry graves in th' mud. Soon t' follow were his crewmates t' th' locker by those that were disinclined t' follow th' ways o' ol' One-Eye. Ambush, plague an' scurvy took their toll on his deckhands. This left our Thunderwrath in a queer quandry, no longer at peace with his former beliefs in ol' One-Eye. After a bout o' solitude with nary but grog fer company, he scarpered back t' his hole in Emauracus, an' challenged th' priests o' One Eye t' a battle o' wits. Nae crew had ever brought mutiny upon th' priests in livin' memory, an' all this was brought down t' them wantin' him gone. But Thunderwrath be stubborn, and in defiance he held his course true. Then usin' some witchcraft he began t' glow an' th' priests saw naught but ol' One-Eye comin' t' this world, if yer inclined t' believe such things. Th' wisest o' th' priests took him down deeper in th' caves t' th' \"holy o' holies\" place. After weeks of journeyin', Thunderwrath found no wayward thinkin's, nor ancient booty, but th' ol' one itself! It were not merely lying dormant in th' rock fer aeons; nae, t'were th' maker itself. Th' One-Eye had crafted th' vast jewel rich shield around it, as protection 'gainst th' nightmares that lay beyond th' sky. An' so, One-Eye reckoned he had created th' land an' th' seas. Aye, Thunderwrath had no reason t' object, given everything else he'd heard that day. Perhaps One-Eye were a lyin' scoundrel, fit only fer th' eighth level o' hell, who be buried deep into a gaol o' stone - perchance he didn't craft anything at all. Thunderwrath had no such doubts in his mind. Despite what ye believe, his restored faith bolsters his might in battle, an' nary a soul can argue 'gainst this."

In a later day an' age, th' Vizier o' Greed, Ptholopthales, erected his \"lodestone ziggurat\" on th' slopes o' th' dead volcano, knowin' all too well that any looters who were a-seekin' his wealth would have t' survive th' spider-haunted passages. After ages o' maternal peace, Black Arachnia found 'erself beset by a steady rut o' theives an' cutpurses, headstrong knights an' noble youths--all o' them delicious, certainly, an' yet tendin' t' make fer a less than nurturin' environment fer th' lass' innocent offsprin'. Tirin' o' th' intrusions, she paid a visit t' Ptholopthales; an' when he were unwillin' t' come t' a compromise, she wrapped th' man up in fine silk an' set 'im aside as t' be th' centerpiece o' a special birthday feast, yarr! That said, missin' th' Magnetic Ziggurat's master made fer an embolden'd generation o' intruders. When one o' th' lass' newborns were trodden underfoot by a clumsy adventurer, now, that were when she reached th' end o' 'er patience. Broodmother headed fer th' surface, declarin' th' lass' intent t' rid th' world o' each an' e'ery possible invader, down t' th' last Admiral that be if needed, 'till she could be sure fer herself that th' lass' nursery might once more be a safe an' innocent sort o' place fer raisin' th' lass' wee tykes."

"DOTA_Tooltip_ability_invoker_ice_wall"	"Ice Wall"
"DOTA_Tooltip_ability_invoker_deafening_blast"	"Ear-Poppin' Blast"
"npc_dota_hero_invoker_bio"	"Arr, 'fore th' rum started t' be passed 'round, magic used t' be quite useful in th' art o' memory. Didn't need no fancy gears or metal or any o' that! All ye needed was a few hums here an' there an' ye've got magic. Th' best mages in those days be those that 'ad a better memory than me Pa, but th' mages couldn't learn everythin', so they had t' split up an' learn diff'rent magicks. Magic be so tough that sometimes ye dun learn more than three spells in yer life, if not four. Yer typical wizards would know jus' two an' they be fine wit' that. Usually used t' make rum, so nothin' t' worry. Mages in some mud huts would probably know one an' forget it th' day th' bugger needs t' use it. Aye, but thar always be a smarty that jus' does everythin' better than th' rest of us! He came t' be know as Th' Invoker, a name that dun look so mean, but it be 'is mind that scares ye. When 'e be a young one, 'e could cast more than ten spells, even at th' same time! Th' Cap'n didn't like silly spells an' jus' forgot 'em so 'e could remember better ones. One o' his most devious spells be th' \"Sempiternal Cantrap\"--or as th' boys call it, th' \"Anti-scurvy\" spell. Th' odd spell makes ye live fer almost ferever, granted if ye ain't crushed t' dust. Most who cast this live by themselves, but Th' Invoker ain't no sissy boy. He goes 'round, prancing 'bout. An' lemme tell ye, 'e makes sure ye know it."

"npc_dota_hero_undying_bio"	"How many shots o' rum has it been since th' Dirge lost his name? Th' ravaged sight o' his mind remembers not.
Dimly he recalls masts an' waves an' th' grimy face o' his first mate. He remembers a raid: pain an' fear as sweaty hands swiped at his side. He remembers terror as his foes threw him in th' sea o' th' Dead God with his crew, t' hear th' Dirge an' be eaten int' th' abyss. In th' dark heart o' th' sea, time left 'em. Thought left 'em. Wits left 'em. Hunger, tho', ripped at 'em. They turn'd on each other, with patch'd eyes an' wooden teeth. Then it came: distant at start, a mere note at th' edge o' hearin', joined by another, then another, unyiedlin' an' unendin'. Th' chorus grew int' a livin' plank o' sound thrustin' in his mind 'til no other idea remained. With th' Dirge consumin' him, he open'd his arms t' th' Dead God an' open'd his mind t' th' thought o' despair. Yet destruction was not what he'd been chosen fer. Th' Dead God demanded war. In th' belly o' th' great nothin', he be grant'd a new purpose: t' spread th' Dirge from sea t' sea, t' rally th' landless dead against th' sealess livin'. He was t' become th' Undyin', th' first mate o' th' Dead God, t' rise an' fall an' rise 'gain whenever his body fail'd him. T' trudge on through death unendin', that th' Dirge might never end."
